[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A Jazzer fuzzing run triggered a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception indicating [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         a remote JNDI lookup within the Log4j logging pipeline. The fuzzer discovered that  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         attacker-controlled JNDI URLs could be passed through Log4j’s `JndiLookup`,         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         potentially leading to remote code execution or sensitive data exfiltration.        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue Manifestation                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The exception stack trace shows the fuzzer invoking Log4j’s lookup mechanism,     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         which ultimately calls into a JNDI lookup hook [1m([0m`NamingContextLookup.lookupHook`[1m)[0m.  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The relevant call chain is:                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             • `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.NamingContextLookup.lookupHook`      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             • `org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup.lookup`                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             • `org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.Interpolator.lookup`                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             • String substitution in `StrSubstitutor`                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             • Message formatting in `MessagePatternConverter` and `PatternLayout`           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             • Appender logic in `AbstractOutputStreamAppender` and `LoggerConfig`           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Vulnerability Type                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The issue is classified as a “Remote JNDI Lookup” vulnerability. Untrusted JNDI   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         lookups [1m([0mCWE-[1;36m668[0m [35m/[0m CWE-[1;36m502[0m[1m)[0m can, depending on the JVM, lead to remote code          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         execution or the exfiltration of sensitive information.                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Important Observations                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The exception is raised by the Jazzer sanitizer when a lookup is performed on   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         an attacker-controlled URL.                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The fuzzer harness [1m([0m`SimpleLoggerFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[1m)[0m only serves as the [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entry point; the risky behavior resides entirely within Log4j’s lookup and          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         formatting logic.                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The stack trace indicates that even a single log invocation can trigger this    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         lookup path if the log message includes a `$[1m{[0mjndi:[33m...[0m[1m}[0m` pattern.                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Code Areas for Investigation                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           To gain a holistic view of this issue, the following components should be         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         reviewed:                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1;36m1[0m. `NamingContextLookup.kt` – the Jazzer hook intercepting JNDI calls           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1;36m2[0m. `org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup` – the implementation of    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the `$[1m{[0mjndi:[33m...[0m[1m}[0m` lookup                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1;36m3[0m. `org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.Interpolator` and `StrSubstitutor` –   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         how variables are resolved and substituted in log messages                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1;36m4[0m. `org.apache.logging.log4j.core.pattern.MessagePatternConverter` [35m/[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `PatternFormatter` [35m/[0m `PatternLayout` – how formatted messages are produced          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             [1;36m5[0m. `org.apache.logging.log4j.core.appender.AbstractOutputStreamAppender` and    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `LoggerConfig` – how log events trigger the lookup during normal operation          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         No assumptions are made here about underlying root causes or fixes. The focus is    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         solely on identifying and describing the remote JNDI lookup vulnerability surfaced  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         by the fuzzer.                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability stems from Log4j’s `JndiLookup` always performing a JNDI [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlookup whenever `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mjndi:[0m[33m...[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` appears in a log message, with no controls on which [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJNDI names or URL schemes are allowed. This lets an attacker supply remote JNDI [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mURLs [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. “ldap:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m…”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and trigger remote code execution or data exfiltration.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Critical Logic[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep the lookup API signature and the integration with [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Interpolator`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`StrSubstitutor` intact so existing pattern-layout and lookup [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmechanisms behave normally for other lookups.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Continue catching `NamingException` to avoid breaking on missing or invalid [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocal entries.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain support for legitimate JNDI lookups in trusted contexts [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. JEE [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontainer “jav[0m[1;92ma:c[0m[39momp/env/…”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Introduce a Feature Flag to Disable JNDI Lookups by Default[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change the static `ENABLE_JNDI` flag in `JndiLookup.java` from a hardcoded [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`true` to a value driven by a system property or configuration parameter [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`log4j2.enableJndiLookup`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, defaulting to `false`.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     * Add a private static initializer method:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       private static final boolean ENABLE_JNDI = [0m[1;35minitEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       private static boolean [0m[1;35minitEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           String prop = [0m[1;35mPropertiesUtil.getProperties[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           [0m[1;35m.getStringProperty[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"log4j2.enableJndiLookup"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"false"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           return [0m[1;35mBoolean.parseBoolean[0m[1;39m([0m[39mprop[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     * Document in release notes and reference manual that users who truly need [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJNDI lookup must explicitly set this property to `true`.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLogEvent, String[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, retain the existing `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey == null || [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m!ENABLE_JNDI[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return null;` check so that lookups are fully disabled by default.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Restrict Remote URL Schemes Even When Enabled[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After converting the raw key to the JNDI name [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, insert[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic to detect and block remote‐scheme lookups:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     String name = [0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Block any URI with a scheme delimiter, e.g. ldap:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m, rmi:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m, dns:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mname.contains[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"://"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Optionally log at DEBUG level that a remote-scheme lookup was blocked.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return null;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Optionally, further restrict to only allow container-local prefixes:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mname.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCONTAINER_JNDI_RESOURCE_PATH_PREFIX[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return null;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     This ensures that only “jav[0m[1;92ma:c[0m[39momp/env/…” names are looked up, blocking all [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremote addresses even when the feature flag is enabled.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.java:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Change `private static boolean ENABLE_JNDI = true;` to a final flag [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitialized via a helper that reads `log4j2.enableJndiLookup` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefault “false”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Immediately after obtaining `[0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, add a check for [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mname.contains[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"://"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, returning `null` to block remote URIs.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Also check for [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`![0m[1;35mname.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCONTAINER_JNDI_RESOURCE_PATH_PREFIX[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` if local-only JNDI is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesired, returning `null`.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Update documentation:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In the reference manual, describe the new system property [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`log4j2.enableJndiLookup`, noting the default `false` behavior and how to re-enable[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafely [0m[1;39m([0m[39monly in trusted environments[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Add release notes highlighting that JNDI lookup is now disabled by default [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto mitigate remote-JNDI exploitation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLog4Shell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Write unit tests:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Confirm that without the property set, `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mjndi:ldap:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/evil/[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` returns [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`null` and does not perform a lookup.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Confirm that `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mjndi:jav[0m[1;92ma:c[0m[39momp/env/jdbc/MyDS[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` still returns the correct [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalue when the property is explicitly enabled and an `InitialContext` entry exists.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Test that setting `log4j2.[0m[33menableJndiLookup[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m` re-enables only local [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlookups.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Justification and Side-Effect Mitigation[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By disabling JNDI lookups by default, we eliminate the untrusted-URL attack [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvector while preserving backward compatibility for environments that explicitly [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menable it.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Blocking `:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m` ensures remote schemes are never accidentally invoked, even if [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe feature flag is misconfigured.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing functionality [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpattern layouts without `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mjndi:[0m[33m...[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`, other lookup [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtypes like `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39menv:…[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is unaffected.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Potential side effect: users relying on remote-JNDI for specific enterprise [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintegrations will need to opt in; this is acceptable given the high security risk.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach mirrors the upstream Log4j [0m[1;36m2.16[0m[39m+ solution which removed/disabled[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJndiLookup by default and reinforces defense-in-depth by restricting URL schemes.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References to Similar Solutions[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Upstream Log4j [0m[1;36m2.16[0m[39m removed JndiLookup entirely; Log4j [0m[1;36m2.15[0m[39m introduced [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`formatMsgNoLookups` and disabled lookups by default.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Our solution follows the same principle—feature-flag disablement plus tight [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mURL-scheme filtering—while maintaining backward-compatibility and configurability.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         An automated fuzzer triggered a critical security alert in Log4j Core’s JndiLookup  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         implementation: it performed a remote JNDI lookup that can lead to remote code      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         execution or data exfiltration. A proposed patch attempted to tie JNDI enablement   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         to a new `log4j2.enableJndiLookup` property, block any lookup string containing     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         “:[35m/[0m[35m/[0m”, and only allow names beginning with the container prefix. After applying the [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         patch, the build failed: the newly introduced `ENABLE_JNDI` field was declared      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `final`, but the existing code still assigns to it, causing a compilation error.    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Exception: `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical:      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Remote JNDI Lookup`                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Stack trace shows the fuzzer exercising                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup.lookup` via a logging call,        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         leading to a remote JNDI URL being resolved.                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Security concern: attacker-controlled JNDI URLs may cause remote code          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         execution or data leaks depending on JVM version.                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The failure was detected by Jazzer during a fuzzing run on a custom            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `SimpleLoggerFuzzer`.                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Important Observations                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The vulnerable code path is `[1;35mJndiLookup.lookup[0m[1m([0mString key[1m)[0m`, which             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         unconditionally performs `new [1;35mInitialContext[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.lookup[0m[1m([0mname[1m)[0m`.                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - No existing configuration flag was observed to disable JNDI lookups entirely.  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The vulnerability surfaces during normal log formatting, through               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `StringSubstitutor` and `PatternLayout`.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Changes to `JndiLookup.java`:                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                ```                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                private static final boolean ENABLE_JNDI = [1;35minitEnableJndi[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                [1m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                ```                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • In `[1;35mlookup[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`:                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                - Compute `name = [1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1m([0mkey[1m)[0m`.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                - If `[1;35mname.contains[0m[1m([0m[32m"://"[0m[1m)[0m`, return null [1m([0mblocking remote URIs[1m)[0m.             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                - If `![1;35mname.startsWith[0m[1m([0mCONTAINER_JNDI_RESOURCE_PATH_PREFIX[1m)[0m`, return null    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0mallow only local JNDI[1m)[0m.                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                - Use `[1;35mctx.lookup[0m[1m([0mname[1m)[0m` instead of calling `[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1m([0mkey[1m)[0m` inline.   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The intent is to allow JNDI lookups only when explicitly enabled via a         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         property, and to prevent remote lookups altogether.                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Patch Result & Build Log                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Build error in `JndiLookup.java` at line [1;36m97[0m, column [1;36m9[0m:                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              “cannot assign a value to final variable ENABLE_JNDI.”                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - This indicates that elsewhere in the class [1m([0mlikely in a setter or static       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         block[1m)[0m code still attempts to reassign `ENABLE_JNDI`, conflicting with its new      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `final` modifier.                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The overall build of `log4j-core` failed, while other modules succeeded.       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. Areas for Further Investigation                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m            - Usage and documentation of the new `log4j2.enableJndiLookup` property: ensure  [2m                [0m
